  <script>
   (function () {
      if ("PerformanceTiming" && "PerformanceObserver" in window) {
          const observer = new PerformanceObserver(function(list) {
              for (const entry of list.getEntries()) {
                  const metricName = entry.name;
                  const time = Math.round(entry.startTime + entry.duration);
                  if (typeof newrelic !== 'undefined') {
                      newrelic.setCustomAttribute(metricName, time);
                  }
              }
          });
          if ("PerformancePaintTiming" in window){observer.observe({entryTypes: ['paint', 'mark', 'measure']});}
          else {observer.observe({entryTypes: ['mark', 'measure']});}
      }
      
      // from https://github.dowjones.net/wsjdn-tesla/dj.svc.end_user_monitor/blob/master/lib/page_perf_monitor.js#L161-L195
      if (window.PerformanceObserver) {
        // Holds current CLS score, as changes over time.
        var _cumulativeLayoutShiftScore = 0;
        // Perf Obserever tracks CLS
        var clsObserver = new PerformanceObserver(function(list) {
          var entries = list.getEntries();
          for (var i=0; i<entries.length;i++) {
            // Only count layout shifts without recent user input.
            if (!entries[i].hadRecentInput) {
              _cumulativeLayoutShiftScore += entries[i].value;
            }
          }
        });
        clsObserver.observe({type: 'layout-shift', buffered: true});
        // Sends the final score to newrelic once when tab change/link change occurs.
        document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', function() {
        if (document.visibilityState === 'hidden') {
          // Force any pending records to be dispatched.
          clsObserver.takeRecords();
          clsObserver.disconnect();
          // Log the final score to the console.
            if (typeof newrelic !== 'undefined') {
              newrelic.setCustomAttribute('layout-shift', _cumulativeLayoutShiftScore);
            }
          // console.log('CLS:', _cumulativeLayoutShiftScore);
        }
        });
      }
    })();
